  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_512a271c-c20d-458b-936d-0e2d649f0e63'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer3651686371315711323">After changing shape several times, the ball eventually turned into a huge face. It floated alongside the air-car. This time, time instead of sending him mental message, the face spoke out aloud and the whole air-car vibrated with its intensity. "If you are foolish enough to renege on your contract, you will be severely punished. For your sake, I hope you wouldn't do such </span>
  <span id="freeText3651686371315711323" style="display:none">After changing shape several times, the ball eventually turned into a huge face. It floated alongside the air-car. This time, time instead of sending him mental message, the face spoke out aloud and the whole air-car vibrated with its intensity. "If you are foolish enough to renege on your contract, you will be severely punished. For your sake, I hope you wouldn't do such a thing." When Tarmy made no attempt to respond, the face turned and pressed itself against the millipede-free window. A moment later, Tarmy felt the fat slug entering his mind, the sign that the face was attempting to use its powers to obtain his response by other means. But as the slug dug deeper, Samantha's cover stories began springing out of the corners of his mind. Instead of obtaining Tarmy's agreement, all that the face saw was a burning army transporter surrounded by bodies. Undeterred, the face continued its assault. Samantha had anticipated that Tarmy might come up against an adept, so the mental images of death and destruction flowed unchecked. After failing to break Tarmy's defences, the face removed the slug and tried reason. "You can't win, Mr Tarleton, so why don't you do yourself a favour and cooperate? It will be better for you in the long run. Now, where is the miniature pulse drive engine?" Tarmy realised why the millipedes hadn't been allowed to attack. It was obvious that the Great Ones were hoping to retrieve the engine. When Tarmy didn't respond, the face said, "I am prepared to overlook your desertion if you agree to tell us where the engine is and also honour your contract by showing us how to convert the engine into a bomb."</span>
  <a data-text-id="3651686371315711323" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2394796157" />
    <a title="Nayab" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29188851-nayab"><img alt="Nayab" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603399043p2/29188851.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2394796157?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nayab" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nayab" href="/user/show/29188851-nayab">Nayab</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36142727-arcadia-s-children">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2394796157" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6913383441627855046"><strong>Captivating!</strong><br/><br/>Some books are hard to put down and end up transporting you to another world. The world of magic and suspense, this book did exactly that. It took me to a magical world, an escape that I always seek whenever I pick up a book. Reading for me is like breathing and a book well-written is an addiction and a weakness. I rarely read sci-fi but this book was most definitely worth it. Arcadia's Children is a sci-fi thriller that kept me hooked till the very end. It was fast-paced and most ce</span>
  <span id="freeText6913383441627855046" style="display:none"><strong>Captivating!</strong><br /><br />Some books are hard to put down and end up transporting you to another world. The world of magic and suspense, this book did exactly that. It took me to a magical world, an escape that I always seek whenever I pick up a book. Reading for me is like breathing and a book well-written is an addiction and a weakness. I rarely read sci-fi but this book was most definitely worth it. Arcadia's Children is a sci-fi thriller that kept me hooked till the very end. It was fast-paced and most certainly would not let you get bored. I couldn't get up without finishing it. There are absolutely no boring moments and is a total page turner and totally recommended if you are into sci-fi or you are looking to try this genre. <br /><br />This is the best book recommendation for people who are new to the genre of science fiction. If you want your friend to join your fandoms from the science fiction world, this is the place to start. I was very pleasantly surprised. This book is exciting, stimulating, and totally captivating. I honestly loved the writing style of the author. It was easy to understand and very smooth. It was just perfect. The writing style and an amazing plotline made it my new favorite and the point of my obsession. <br /><br />The plot twist left me staring at a wall, mesmerized. This book is exactly what I need, after all, who could say no to such an exceptional read? It was thrilling and fascinating. I really enjoyed reading the book, one of the reasons being an amazing writing style; easy to understand and flawless. It is extremely hard to find a book that is worth your money anymore, this would totally make every single penny worth it. This is the book you can put on your shelf and cherish it forever. I wouldn’t think twice rereading it. It is very rare that I reread a book but this, I definitely would, without a second thought.<br />This book would totally captivate you and take your place. Careful, it'll keep you up all night, totally hooked but be assured; it would be totally worth it. If you are looking for book recommendations to gift to a book lover, this book would be your perfect option. I received it as a gift and trust me, I really could not ask for more. It is pure perfection and made my birthday really special. I am sure your book lover friend would totally fall in love with it. I am desperately waiting for the sequel. This book is totally worth your money and your time and you most definitely won't regret it. This is one of those books that you can proudly make a part of your collection in your library and take it out every now and then. I rarely reread books, but I am unable to put it back on the shelf just yet.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12292861504830517505">Arcadia’s Children: Samantha’s Revenge is a promising series debut, challenging and addictive. Throughout the novel readers will get the sense they are in the hands of an author who has built a deep world of wonder. Another part of Williams’ success here is how he is able to casually world-build by giving us an immersive experience where the magic of the technology we encounter, so very alien to what we know, is lived and thus explained by character actions. It may be, for some, overwhelming at </span>
  <span id="freeText12292861504830517505" style="display:none">Arcadia’s Children: Samantha’s Revenge is a promising series debut, challenging and addictive. Throughout the novel readers will get the sense they are in the hands of an author who has built a deep world of wonder. Another part of Williams’ success here is how he is able to casually world-build by giving us an immersive experience where the magic of the technology we encounter, so very alien to what we know, is lived and thus explained by character actions. It may be, for some, overwhelming at first but soon the tone of the novel brings readers around facilitated by a prose that is easy and quick. <br /><br />read full review: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://misanthropester.com/2018/06/03/arcadias-children-samanthas-revenge-by-andrew-r-williams/">https://misanthropester.com/2018/06/0...</a></span>

  <span id="freeText3439145352502585964" style="display:none">I was in the mood for a different sci-fic this weekend so picked up this book by Andrew R Williams after a friend recommended it to me.   <span id="freeText14003106192285212952" style="display:none">Don't get the wrong idea about this futuristic sci-fi book. Williams (Author) constructs a story about a shape-shifter and AI humanoid who has vengeance. The potential for destruction of the world is always a risk in these novels. Afterall, AI is often programmed one way and acts in another way. It's a battle between the heroes and villains. Those characters fighting through the worlds with leaders who have no qualms at refusing justice for mayhem. <br /><br />Drawn into a world that is is a stretch to my imagination and acceptance since sci-fi usually is not my flavor of reading. But I'm attending a sci-fi book group and it was suggested I sample Andrew Williams series to become more at ease with developing situations, shapeshifters, sorcery and action. <br />This is not the first book in the series in fact, you may want to flash back to Arcadia's Children to embrace the full plot and energy behind the author convincingly, skillfully, master novel. </span>

<div id="review_3059474203" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3059474203" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3059474203?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3059474203" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2043698978565602375">Absorbing, challenging – and addictive! A very fine Sci-Fi novel<br/><br/>British author Andrew R. Williams has written an impressive array of books, from fantasy fiction, such as this ongoing series ARCADIA’S CHILDREN, to architectural information books – DOMESTIC BUILDING SURVEYS, PRACTICAL GUIDE TO ALTERATIONS AND EXTENSIONS, and A PRACTICAL GUIDE TO SINGLE STOREY HOUSE EXTENSIONS. He is a chartered surveyor.<br/><br/>The intricacies of Andrew’s attention to detail make this novel as accessible, and even credibl</span>
  <span id="freeText2043698978565602375" style="display:none">Absorbing, challenging – and addictive! A very fine Sci-Fi novel<br /><br />British author Andrew R. Williams has written an impressive array of books, from fantasy fiction, such as this ongoing series ARCADIA’S CHILDREN, to architectural information books – DOMESTIC BUILDING SURVEYS, PRACTICAL GUIDE TO ALTERATIONS AND EXTENSIONS, and A PRACTICAL GUIDE TO SINGLE STOREY HOUSE EXTENSIONS. He is a chartered surveyor.<br /><br />The intricacies of Andrew’s attention to detail make this novel as accessible, and even credible, as the initial book in this series – ARCADIA’S CHILDREN: SAMANTHA’S REVENGE. Andrew knows the realm of imagination and uses his mastery of the science fiction genre in a manner that few authors can match. Wildly inventive concepts and description of events and forms become clearly relatable in his hands. A hint of why Andrew’s bizarre world works so well is evident in his offering ‘facts’ about Arcadian archaeology before the story’s onset. For instance, Arcadia is the third planet in the Salus System. As it is in a Goldilocks Zone, the planet is an Earth type, and The Wreck - Although badly damaged, The Wreck is still being subjected to close scrutiny. It has also become a major tourist attraction. Since teleportation systems were installed, over two million tourists per annum visit The Wreck. When entering a strange realm such preparation makes the journey more credible.<br /><br />As an overview of where this series will take us, Andrew opens this book with the following – ‘After changing shape several times, the ball eventually turned into a huge face. It floated alongside the air-car. This time, time instead of sending him mental message, the face spoke out aloud and the whole air-car vibrated with its intensity. “If you are foolish enough to renege on your contract, you will be severely punished. For your sake, I hope you wouldn’t do such a thing.” When Tarmy made no attempt to respond, the face turned and pressed itself against the millipede-free window. A moment later, Tarmy felt the fat slug entering his mind, the sign that the face was attempting to use its powers to obtain his response by other means. But as the slug dug deeper, Samantha’s cover stories began springing out of the corners of his mind. Instead of obtaining Tarmy’s agreement, all that the face saw was a burning army transporter surrounded by bodies. Undeterred, the face continued its assault. Samantha had anticipated that Tarmy might come up against an adept, so the mental images of death and destruction flowed unchecked. After failing to break Tarmy’s defenses, the face removed the slug and tried reason. “You can’t win, Mr. Tarleton, so why don’t you do yourself a favour and cooperate? It will be better for you in the long run. Now, where is the miniature pulse drive engine?” Tarmy realized why the millipedes hadn’t been allowed to attack. It was obvious that the Great Ones were hoping to retrieve the engine. When Tarmy didn’t respond, the face said, “I am prepared to overlook your desertion if you agree to tell us where the engine is and also honour your contract by showing us how to convert the engine into a bomb.’ Simply superb writing!<br /><br />Keen characterizations create near visible images and the plot of the story is full of imaginative excursions and strange events. Exciting and beautifully realized, this is one of the better Sci-Fi fantasy novels of the day. Recommended. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2043698978565602375" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2684967451182941291">This is a very captivating sci-fi fantasy story that will keep you reading until you have finished the last page. The story is one of a kind. You will want to read more. But alas the story will be over. <br/><br/>Williams’ sci-fi fantasy story has many intriguing twists and turns which will easily captivate your attention from the beginning. Williams portrays an exciting and adventurous story of alien invasion in a vivid and convincing way. <br/><br/>In addition, the characters are drawn with amazing credibility, d</span>
  <span id="freeText2684967451182941291" style="display:none">This is a very captivating sci-fi fantasy story that will keep you reading until you have finished the last page. The story is one of a kind. You will want to read more. But alas the story will be over. <br /><br />Williams’ sci-fi fantasy story has many intriguing twists and turns which will easily captivate your attention from the beginning. Williams portrays an exciting and adventurous story of alien invasion in a vivid and convincing way. <br /><br />In addition, the characters are drawn with amazing credibility, depth, and integrity. If you’re looking for an action packed, sci-fi fantasy adventure that’s packed with courage, bravery and heroism that will have you sitting on the edge of your seat, this book is for you.<br /><br />Further, the story had every element a good story should have. This amazing story has an exciting plot, attention to detail, but best of all fleshed out, well-written and well-rounded character development. There’s also an abundance of well-illustrated scenes that will make you feel like you are right in the middle of the story in another worldly place, far away from the here and now. <br /><br />There is something very magical about reading fantasy fiction like this. It helps us imagine worlds that are quite removed from our own and some of the possibilities outside our realm of the normal of here and now. And this story did exactly that for me. <br /><br />This is the first book in the series. I can’t wait to see what Andrew Williams comes up next. I’m sure he’s creating it as we speak. <br /></span>

<div id="review_3061073149" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer5480556399087456505">Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge is an excellent sci-fi novel by the established author, Andrew R Williams. The book has elements of several genres in it, with the most prevalent being science-fiction and fantasy. <br/><br/>Williams is an excellent world-builder and the world he builds in this book is one that the reader can’t help but get lost in. His detailed characters and world-building really help you feel as though you are a part of the novel and once you open those first few pages, you won’t </span>
  <span id="freeText5480556399087456505" style="display:none">Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge is an excellent sci-fi novel by the established author, Andrew R Williams. The book has elements of several genres in it, with the most prevalent being science-fiction and fantasy. <br /><br />Williams is an excellent world-builder and the world he builds in this book is one that the reader can’t help but get lost in. His detailed characters and world-building really help you feel as though you are a part of the novel and once you open those first few pages, you won’t be able to put the book down anytime soon. <br /><br />The book’s central narrative is also brilliant, expertly working in elements from several different genres. The writing is also incredibly compact and the book flies along at an excellent pace. <br /><br />Arcadia's Children: Samantha’s Revenge is the ideal book for those who like their books to be slightly more fantastical and experimental and who want to explore a whole new world. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5480556399087456505" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2415733657" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2415733657" />
    <a title="Píaras Cíonnaoíth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22641397-p-aras-c-onnao-th"><img alt="Píaras Cíonnaoíth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515739292p2/22641397.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2415733657?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Píaras Cíonnaoíth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Píaras Cíonnaoíth" href="/user/show/22641397-p-aras-c-onnao-th">Píaras Cíonnaoíth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36142727-arcadia-s-children">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2415733657" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5814601907156928170">A well-crafted sci-fi fantasy that’s left open for exciting sequels!<br/><br/>Author Andrew R. Williams weaves an outstanding and noteworthy tale of sci-fi fantasy with intriguing twists and turns that will easily captivate the reader’s attention from the beginning. The author paints an exciting and adventurous story of alien invasion in a very vivid and convincing way. In addition, the characters are drawn with great credibility and integrity. If you’re looking for an action packed, sci-fi fantasy advent</span>
  <span id="freeText5814601907156928170" style="display:none">A well-crafted sci-fi fantasy that’s left open for exciting sequels!<br /><br />Author Andrew R. Williams weaves an outstanding and noteworthy tale of sci-fi fantasy with intriguing twists and turns that will easily captivate the reader’s attention from the beginning. The author paints an exciting and adventurous story of alien invasion in a very vivid and convincing way. In addition, the characters are drawn with great credibility and integrity. If you’re looking for an action packed, sci-fi fantasy adventure that’s packed to the rafters with courage, bravery and heroism, this book has it all…and more.<br /><br />The story had every element a good story should have. An exciting plot, attention to detail, but best of all fleshed out, well-written and well-rounded character development. There’s an abundance of well-illustrated scenes that make you feel like you are right there in the story, and that’s something I really look for in a good book.<br /><br />There is something very magical about reading fantasy fiction. It speaks to the very thread of my imagination, jolting it to life and transporting it on an exhilarating journey. This story did exactly that, leaving me captivated as I was introduced to a new world and mesmerizing characters. It appears to be the author’s debut novel in this genre and I just have to say that it was a book that fans of the YA and Fantasy genre will not be disappointed in. I truly believe that the author has the potential to weave even more magic for future readers of this series.<br /><br />The book description gives a preview: ‘After changing shape several times, the ball eventually turned into a huge face. It floated alongside the air-car. This time instead of sending him mental message, the face spoke out aloud and the whole air-car vibrated with its intensity. “If you are foolish enough to renege on your contract, you will be severely punished. For your sake, I hope you wouldn’t do such a thing.”<br /><br />When Tarmy made no attempt to respond, the face turned and pressed itself against the millipede-free window. A moment later, Tarmy felt the fat slug entering his mind, the sign that the face was attempting to use its powers to obtain his response by other means. But as the slug dug deeper, Samantha’s cover stories began springing out of the corners of his mind. Instead of obtaining Tarmy’s agreement, all that the face saw was a burning army transporter surrounded by bodies. Undeterred, the face continued its assault. Samantha had anticipated that Tarmy might come up against an adept, so the mental images of death and destruction flowed unchecked.<br /><br />After failing to break Tarmy’s defenses, the face removed the slug and tried reason. “You can’t win, Mr. Tarleton, so why don’t you do yourself a favour and cooperate? It will be better for you in the long run. Now, where is the miniature pulse drive engine?”<br /><br />Tarmy realized why the millipedes hadn’t been allowed to attack. It was obvious that the Great Ones were hoping to retrieve the engine. When Tarmy didn’t respond, the face said, “I am prepared to overlook your desertion if you agree to tell us where the engine is and also honour your contract by showing us how to convert the engine into a bomb.”<br /><br />Now, if that’s not enough to whet your appetite, I don’t know what will. But if you want to find out what happens, you’ll just have to turn the pages for yourself! However, I will say it was well worth the read. It’s my first time reading this author and I must say I was very impressed.<br /><br />Captivating and commendable, this work had me immersed from the beginning. The story flowed from scene to scene with ease, and the author shows exceptional ability when it comes to storytelling. There are plenty of attention-grabbing moments in this page turner that will take the reader on a truly spellbinding journey!<br /><br />It’s one of those books that comes along occasionally that makes you want to read it non-stop until you get to the end. I’m giving nothing further away here. And this, I hope, will only add to the mystery and enjoyment for the reader.<br /><br />If this volume is anything to go by, I’ll certainly be looking forward to reading more from Andrew R. Williams in the future. This has all the hallmarks of making a great series. I would definitely recommend this book and would love to see it adapted for the Silver Screen. I honestly think it would make a fantastic movie or TV series. A well-deserved five stars. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5814601907156928170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10688231497531821126">I was in the mood for some sci-fi as it was a while since I’d read any. Instead of going for one of the more mainstream titles I wanted to give something different a try, and was intrigued by this book from Andrew R. Williams. It was the cover that initially caused me to pause and read more as it has a certain surreal quality to it, but the blurb was enough to win me over and give it a read. Williams has created an extraordinary world with some very vivid imagery and a compelling, but not unnece</span>
  <span id="freeText10688231497531821126" style="display:none">I was in the mood for some sci-fi as it was a while since I’d read any. Instead of going for one of the more mainstream titles I wanted to give something different a try, and was intrigued by this book from Andrew R. Williams. It was the cover that initially caused me to pause and read more as it has a certain surreal quality to it, but the blurb was enough to win me over and give it a read. Williams has created an extraordinary world with some very vivid imagery and a compelling, but not unnecessarily complicated sci-fi story. I hate when authors get bogged down in minutiae in science fiction. But that isn’t the case here.<br /><br />All in all a very enjoyable read and I’ll progress with book two at a later date. <br /></span>

<div id="review_2393134470" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

<div id="review_3083572761" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3083572761" />
    <a title="Red Apple" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/106748550-red-apple"><img alt="Red Apple" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576251870p2/106748550.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3083572761?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Red Apple" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Red Apple" href="/user/show/106748550-red-apple">Red Apple</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3083572761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13977815537512617231">I really enjoyed this book while I was reading it this last week of November. I was drawn in by the plot and mainly because it featured a diva humanoid who held the power to control her realm and those who she selects from differing locations to do her dirty work. Her name is Samantha and she is the leader of a company called Minton Mining Company who owns Arden, the main moon of Arcadia the planet in which this book is entirely about. Add to her intriguing factor are two characters who come wit</span>
  <span id="freeText13977815537512617231" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this book while I was reading it this last week of November. I was drawn in by the plot and mainly because it featured a diva humanoid who held the power to control her realm and those who she selects from differing locations to do her dirty work. Her name is Samantha and she is the leader of a company called Minton Mining Company who owns Arden, the main moon of Arcadia the planet in which this book is entirely about. Add to her intriguing factor are two characters who come with their own wits and strengths, them being: Mick Tarmy, a former police officer and Claire Hyndman who Samantha resurrected from her own devious plans just for the occasion of fighting what are known to be the Great Ones of Arden.<br /><br />This book amazed me with the vast scientific knowledge that its author uses to form his plot and his robotic, humanoid characters. The fact that he knows the terms and details to tell this Sci-fi tale of his proves he knows a lot about the subject he writes about and that is to me an A+. My favorite character is Claire Hyndman because of her special abilities to morph into any kind of persona. She also has a lot of strength and flexibility in her to fight her enemies. I also like the fact that she has a little robot for a friend who is also her bodyguard who looks after her when she is in the middle of battle. This is the kind of book that has a “sorry” front cover but its contents are amazing and entertaining. I judged this book by its cover and I feel ashamed of myself for that. I disliked the cover but when I read into the middle of the book I was definitely enticed into its world of advanced technology and uniformity. While I was reading it I felt like I was watching a movie like Star Wars or the early 80s “V: The Final Battle.” There was absolutely no sexuality in this book and that is a great thing because it was a Sci-fi book. It would feel strange to watch characters in space having some of that because I always felt that astronauts and the sort don’t need sex due to their attire and the lack of gravity in outerspace…haha! My final comments about this book is that I hope it gets the credit its due for being such a well-thought out story by this yet diamond in the rough author. Good job Mr. Williams!<br /><br />I recommend this beauty to those who love a very well-written sci-fi story. It is also a great book to introduce this genre to those who may find it to be kind of hard to grasp, like me. I think for those of you who are into movies like Star Wars, Star Trek, and Starship Troopers, to don’t overlook this one because you will definitely miss out! Like I mentioned above, I had thought this book would be boring and dry and therefore approached it with walls around me but by the middle of it, I was up cheering and rooting for the good guys to bring home the bacon! I am going to say this and I’m saying it with a bang: I enjoyed this book so much you need to take my word for it and get it! Yes! Don’t be late to the game!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13977815537512617231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14406705840101838133">This sci-fi fantasy story has many twists and turns throughout and grabbed my attention right from the beginning. Williams has poured so much imagination into it with phenomenal attention to detail. If you are looking to binge read for a few hours then this is definitely the novel for you, and from my perspective the only time I could put it down was when I finished it. I thoroughly enjoyed the read and have recommended it to all the bookworms I know. Great job.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3088515683" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3088515683?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ground Breaking" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ground Breaking" href="/user/show/106915444-ground-breaking">Ground Breaking</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3088515683" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6592512764924206914">Don't get the wrong idea about this futuristic sci-fi book. Williams (Author) constructs a story about a shape-shifter and AI humanoid who has vengeance. The potential for destruction of the world is always a risk in these novels. Afterall, AI is often programmed one way and acts in another way. It's a battle between the heroes and villains. Those characters fighting through the worlds with leaders who have no qualms at refusing justice for mayhem.<br/>Drawn into a world that is is a stretch to my im</span>
  <span id="freeText6592512764924206914" style="display:none">Don't get the wrong idea about this futuristic sci-fi book. Williams (Author) constructs a story about a shape-shifter and AI humanoid who has vengeance. The potential for destruction of the world is always a risk in these novels. Afterall, AI is often programmed one way and acts in another way. It's a battle between the heroes and villains. Those characters fighting through the worlds with leaders who have no qualms at refusing justice for mayhem.<br />Drawn into a world that is is a stretch to my imagination and acceptance since sci-fi usually is not my flavor of reading. But I'm attending a sci-fi book group and it was suggested I sample Andrew Williams series to become more at ease with developing situations, shapeshifters, sorcery and action.<br />This is not the first book in the series in fact, you may want to flash back to Arcadia's Children to embrace the full plot and energy behind the author convincingly, skillfully, master novel.<br /></span>

<div id="review_3055274164" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3055274164" />
    <a title="Pegboard" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard"><img alt="Pegboard" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498516338p2/47722544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3055274164?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pegboard" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pegboard" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard">Pegboard</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3055274164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11848086049911325113">I found Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge a full-package science fiction. The fantasy and unusual conspiracies within the story makes this a suspense adventure that will keep the reader spellbound. Andrew R. Williams takes you to worlds unknown with technology that is only a dream in the author's mind. Claire Hyndman is would be my favorite character as she morphs into any character she wants. She adds a unique personality to the book. <br/><br/>Andrew R. Williams knows how to spin a story that will </span>
  <span id="freeText11848086049911325113" style="display:none">I found Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge a full-package science fiction. The fantasy and unusual conspiracies within the story makes this a suspense adventure that will keep the reader spellbound. Andrew R. Williams takes you to worlds unknown with technology that is only a dream in the author's mind. Claire Hyndman is would be my favorite character as she morphs into any character she wants. She adds a unique personality to the book. <br /><br />Andrew R. Williams knows how to spin a story that will make you lose sight of your own world. For some reason I read Arcadia's Children: The Fyfield Plantation before Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge. Each book can be read alone, but they are best read in order. The characters are rich, with bountiful personalities. I found Samantha's Revenge entreating from the beginning as a team escapes the clutches of Minton Mining Company. Science fiction fanatics will love this novel, and series. Be sure to set aside a block of time to finish this book since it is hard to put down. <br /></span>

<div id="review_3151598688" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3151598688" />
    <a title="Cup and Saucer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/108798963-cup-and-saucer"><img alt="Cup and Saucer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579176005p2/108798963.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3151598688?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cup and Saucer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cup and Saucer" href="/user/show/108798963-cup-and-saucer">Cup and Saucer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3151598688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5459613845051571808">If you enjoy the Sci-Fi novels of Iain M. Banks then 'Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge' by Andrew R. Williams is a book that you're sure to enjoy. The levels of imagination of the author are off the chart, but he has such a great attention to detail, that you can visualise the weird and wonderful worlds and entities he describes to you.<br/><br/>A shape-shifter and a psychic ex-cop are brought together by Samantha – and AI humanoid intent on revenge. Her quest for revenge may bring an end to the uni</span>
  <span id="freeText5459613845051571808" style="display:none">If you enjoy the Sci-Fi novels of Iain M. Banks then 'Arcadia's Children: Samantha's Revenge' by Andrew R. Williams is a book that you're sure to enjoy. The levels of imagination of the author are off the chart, but he has such a great attention to detail, that you can visualise the weird and wonderful worlds and entities he describes to you.<br /><br />A shape-shifter and a psychic ex-cop are brought together by Samantha – and AI humanoid intent on revenge. Her quest for revenge may bring an end to the universe, troubled ex-cop Tarmy and the resurrected Claire Hyndman can thwart her plans.<br /><br />It is fantastical, engrossing, gripping, exciting, and creepy. It has everything a good Sci-Fi novel needs and then some. It's unpredictable and fantastical, with plot twists I never saw coming. I would love to see this brought the the big or small screen, but until that happens, I will move on to the next in the series.<br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3173902883" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3173902883" />
    <a title="Honey Bee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/109643806-honey-bee"><img alt="Honey Bee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580727468p2/109643806.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3173902883?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Honey Bee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Honey Bee" href="/user/show/109643806-honey-bee">Honey Bee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3173902883" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer412431333600499652">A shape-shifting mind-bending thriller that kept me hooked from the first chapter. Williams is now one of my favorite up-and-coming fantasy / science fiction authors and I’ll avidly await his future releases. The characters were fully developed which is something you don’t always find with smaller press publishing house authors. So much so that I’m sure I have missed out on some side-plot complexities on my first read, so I’ll be going back to reread in a while from now. I would definitely recom</span>
  <span id="freeText412431333600499652" style="display:none">A shape-shifting mind-bending thriller that kept me hooked from the first chapter. Williams is now one of my favorite up-and-coming fantasy / science fiction authors and I’ll avidly await his future releases. The characters were fully developed which is something you don’t always find with smaller press publishing house authors. So much so that I’m sure I have missed out on some side-plot complexities on my first read, so I’ll be going back to reread in a while from now. I would definitely recommend giving this a read for any fans of the sci-fi / fantasy genres.</span>
  <a data-text-id="412431333600499652" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('28m9akEUEN8m7oiNNVE5ztsc+Nb9fv+2NWRJxfPtsSaXhyzjuyLVvGnV7lgTEvaFnqi537O0EHf+gDhKlWVYrg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SLdR3U5FjuQktkHk80JRVw5SnpF79NqdE2j1rPppSyAE+cBUtHNLh2uNJzHVAZ4cS+bfmDU+NVzYjIQjnOGiqA==')})
  }

When he isn't writing, or chartering surveyoring, Andrew spends time with his wife Geraldine, staring up at the stars, and plotting eventual world domination. Don't let that calm demeanour and easy smile fool you, oh no.</span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/55735831-samantha-s-revenge-arcadia-s-children-1">Quotes from Samantha&#39;s Revenge</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;After changing shape several times, the ball eventually turned into a huge face. It floated alongside the air-car. This time, time instead of sending him a mental message, the face spoke out aloud and the whole air-car vibrated with its intensity. “If you are foolish enough to renege on your contract, you will be severely punished. For your sake, I hope you wouldn’t do such a thing.” When Tarmy made no attempt to respond, the face turned and pressed itself against the millipede-free window. A moment later, Tarmy felt the fat slug entering his mind, the sign that the face was attempting to use its powers to obtain his response by other means. But as the slug dug deeper, Samantha’s cover stories began springing out of the corners of his mind. Instead of obtaining Tarmy’s agreement, all that the face saw was a burning army transporter surrounded by bodies. Undeterred, the face continued its assault. Samantha had anticipated that Tarmy might come up against an adept, so the mental images of death and destruction flowed unchecked. After failing to break Tarmy’s defences, the face removed the slug and tried reason. “You can’t win, Mr Tarleton, so why don’t you do yourself a favour and cooperate? It will be better for you in the long run. Now, where is the miniature pulse drive engine?” Tarmy realised why the millipedes hadn’t been allowed to attack. It was obvious that the Great Ones were hoping to retrieve the engine. When Tarmy didn’t respond, the face said, “I am prepared to overlook your desertion if you agree to tell us where the engine is and also honour your contract by showing us how to convert the engine into a bomb.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/10055558-after-changing-shape-several-times-the-ball-eventually-turned-into">75 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Coming back, he took the tracker out of Morley’s hand, slid back into the car and flipped a switch. An internal Mannheim, a force shield, flared into life, dividing the front of the car from the rear. Once he was satisfied the Mannheim would prevent the sound of their voices being picked up by any undiscovered bugs he spoke. “I have a plan, a way to turn the tables on them.”<br /> “How?” Instead of explaining, Lieges waved his hand at the stray dog. Thinking it was going to be fed, the mutt came over. Lieges grabbed it, removed some of the gum he was chewing, fixed the bug to it and stuck the gum under the dog’s collar. Picking the dog up, he placed it in the front of the air-car. <br />Morley hissed. “What the hell are you doing?” <br />“Thinking laterally,” Lieges replied. “We’ll fly a few kilometres from here and push the dog out. The BlackClads will then lock onto the dog and not us. No doubt they’ll realise something is wrong after they’ve been tracking it for a while, but it will probably buy us some time.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/10055563-coming-back-he-took-the-tracker-out-of-morley-s-hand">43 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
